The Rotary Rose Parade Float Committee, Inc. has been promoting Rotary to the world since 1980. This year's float, "Planting the Seeds of Service," celebrates the difference Rotary makes every day in their work to promote peace, fight disease &amp; provide clean water to communities.
Led by Sheriff Jim McDonnell, the Los Angeles County Sheriff's Department Mounted Enforcement Detail rides in their third Rose Parade. #RoseParade
The Tournament of Roses honors the 2017 Rose Bowl Hall of fame inductees, Mack Brown, Cade McNown, Dr. Charles West and Charles Woodson. All inductees are honored with a plaque that includes their name and year of induction at the Court of Champions at the Rose Bowl Stadium.
Northwestern Mutuals philanthropic focus is on accelerating the search for a cure to childhood cancer. Their 2018 #RoseParade float celebrates the joy of being a child through the unforgettable experience of summer camp, while shining a spotlight on stories of incredible patients
Proudly depicting the school name and team colors of one of the outstanding football teams that will compete in the College Football Playoff Semifinal at the Rose Bowl Game, this float presented by Northwestern Mutual jump starts the excitement and support among football fans.
@cityofhope is transforming the future of health and "Making A Difference" in the lives of millions of people around the world. Their float, "Transforming Lives with Hope," reflects the journey each patient makes on the road to recovery. #RoseParade
Ramona, California's official outdoor play, is celebrating its 95th season of performing the nation's longest-running play. Each year, the cast of Ramona takes audiences back to the 1800's through their performance of the play based on the book Ramona. #RoseParade
Australia's Marching Koalas was formed in 1982 when the Arcadia High School Marching Band paid a visit to Newcastle as part of a Sister City relationship. With no American style marching bands in Australia, they decided to form such a band from students attending local schools
The diversity of these animals represents the diversity of the Cal Poly rose float team, which consists of students from both Cal Poly San Luis Obispo and Cal Poly Pomona. #RoseParade
The Cal Poly Universities float, "Dreams Take Flight," inspires the audience to take flight into the childhood dream of these three young energetic animals. #RoseParade
The 100th Rose Queen, Queen Isabella Marie Marez, and the 2018 Royal Court-Alexandra Marie Artura, Savannah Rose Bradley, Lauren Elizabeth Buehner, Georgia Jane Cervenka, Julianne Elise Launstein, and Sydney Grace Pickering-are presented beneath a decorative bejeweled crown.
For the 38th year in a row, the Pasadena City College Herald Trumpets announces the Tournament of Roses Rose Queen and her Royal Court. The band is comprised of an elite group of nine trumpeters and on drummer. #RoseParade
@Scotts_MGro float, "150 Years and Growing" celebrates the beauty and diversity found in backyards across America. From whimsical pollinator gardens to backyard bar-b-ques, this year's float showcases an abundance of colorful floral displays. #RoseParade
This year, @WeAreFarmers is honoring all brave first responders with a parade float entitled, "Honoring Hometown Heroes." The float features a vintage, convertible command chief vehicle followed by a classic red fire truck. #RoseParade
Los Hermanos Ba√±uelos is an authentic Mexican Charro Team that resides in Altadena, California. This year, the 13 riders venture down the 5.5 mile parade route for the 10th time. Each of the horses are owned and cared for by the individual riders. #RoseParade
The City of Alhambra believes that libraries are capable of "Making A Difference" in the community they serve, which is why they've chosen to represent "Story Time" in their float. #RoseParade
The Ronald Reagan High School Band is marching in the #RoseParade for the first time. Within four years of opening in 1999, the band was recognized as a premier marching ensemble, earning multiple Bands of America Regional Championship titles.
The South Pasadena float honors the members of Booster Clubs all over the U.S. for "Making A Difference" in their efforts to support student athletes. The float depicts a group of rambunctious revelers in their vintage roadster on the way to support their team. #RoseParade
The Kyoto Tachibana High School is located in Kyoto Fushimi-ku near Uji, about half-way between Kyoto and Osaka. This is the band's second time marching in the #RoseParade and they are best known for their marching style which includes a continuous dance-style movement.
@WesternAsset is one of the world's leading asset managers, with $429 billion in assets under management across 5 continents and a singular focus on fixed-income since 1971. This year's float, "Oceans of Possibility," features two smiling dolphins as they lead a school of fish.
The horses of Scripps Miramar Ranch trot down the #RoseParade route for the 33rd year. This year Michele Macfarlane and her eye-catching pinto horses will transport the audience to their favorite Western movie.
The 1929 Packard Model 633 transports Lance Tibet, President of the Tournament of Roses, and his family along the parade route. Released in 1929, the 633 was powered by Packard's new 'Standard Eight' engine. #RoseParade
Kaiser Permanente's 2018 Tournament of Roses float entry, "Inspiring Healthy Communities," embodies this year's parade theme and speaks to our mission of Making A Difference to help improve the health of our members and the communities in which we live, work and play. #RoseParade
Founded in 2008 by Mychon Bowen, The Norco Cowgirls Rodeo Drill Team is a professional team of women that perform daring maneuvers at a gallop to thrill the cheering rodeo fans. The girls range in age from 11 to 17 and this will be their third year in the #RoseParade.
This year, the Albertville High School "Aggie" Band marches down Colorado Boulevard for the second time. With nearly 300 students, including the Southern Stars Danceline and Aggie Color Guard, the "Aggie" Band makes up 25% of the high school's population. #RoseParade
China Airlines is a Taiwan-based company that provides the air transportation for passengers &amp; cargo services at a global level. For their 31st #RoseParade float, they have chosen to bring awareness to the importance of protecting our oceans with their float, "Caring for Our Sea"
With a float themed "Sharing Nature's Bounty," Dole celebrates the importance of "Making A Difference" by serving as stewards of the Earth and providing fresh, healthy food to undeserved communities through their partnership with @FeedingAmerica and FOOD Share. #RoseParade
The @WellsFargo stagecoach represents 166 years of American history. This year's stagecoach riders are a testament to the company's commitment to making a difference in the lives of its team members, customers and communities. #RoseParade
The Marching Wildcat Band from Louisburg, Kansas kicks off their city's 150th anniversary by marching in their first #RoseParade. The band comprises more than one-fourth the entire student body and has been led by the same band director, Mr. John Cisetti, for 39 years.
The City of Torrance celebrates their 63rd float in the #RoseParade by bringing awareness to the Madrona Marsh Preserve, an urban oasis in their city which boasts over 1000 species of rare animals and plants.
Mini Therapy Horses is an all-volunteer, non-profit charity that provides therapeutic benefits to children and adults through equine-assisted activities (EAA) and equine-assisted therapy (EAT), leading to greater physical, mental, and emotional well-being. #RoseParade
